           <div class="module has-bottom-divider">
            <section class="media-item">
             <div class="media-item__summary size--large">
              <header class="summary-header">
               <p class="category">
                <a class="js-tealium-tracking" data-tracking="mpos=center&amp;mid=b_top_hero&amp;lindex=1&amp;lcol=item_solo" href="https://www.politico.com/news/elections" target="_blank">
                 Elections
                </a>
               </p>
              </header>
              <h3 class="headline">
               <a class="js-tealium-tracking" data-tracking="mpos=center&amp;mid=b_top_hero&amp;lindex=1&amp;lcol=item_solo" href="https://www.politico.com/news/2021/03/08/gop-sen-roy-blunt-will-not-run-for-reelection-474342" target="_top">
                Sen. Roy Blunt won't run for reelection in latest blow to GOP
               </a>
              </h3>
              <p class="dek">
               The veteran Missouri lawmaker is the fifth Republican incumbent to say he won't be on the ballot next year.
              </p>
              <div class="meta">
               <div class="meta__details">
                <p class="authors">
                 By
                 <span class="vcard">
                  <a class="url fn js-tealium-tracking" data-tracking="mpos=center&amp;mid=b_top_hero&amp;lindex=1&amp;lcol=item_solo" href="https://www.politico.com/staff/andrew-desiderio" rel="author" target="_top">
                   Andrew Desiderio
                  </a>
                 </span>
                </p>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
             <div class="media-item__image">
              <div class="media-item__image-wrapper">
               <a class="js-tealium-tracking" data-tracking="mpos=center&amp;mid=b_top_hero&amp;lindex=1&amp;lcol=item_solo" href="https://www.politico.com/news/2021/03/08/gop-sen-roy-blunt-will-not-run-for-reelection-474342" target="_top">
